 yah shiksha hi to manushya ko pashuon se alag banaati he

 2
 Brahmaji created the creation of Saraswati, when Brahmaji saw the earth silent and dull, he sprinkled water with his kamandal

 Saraswati became the reason for Kumbhakarna sleep, Kumbhakarna did austerities in Govarna for ten thousand years to get the goddess

 The Reserve Bank has issued strict instructions to all banks to protect digital payments from e-fraud after the central government's efforts to move the country towards cashless economy
 rigerv bank ne un sabhi bainkon ko bina vilamb kiye indian computer immergency respos team (cert-in) se vishesh audit karaane kaa aadesh diya he
 After this, on the basis of audit report, instructions have been given to take necessary steps for safety
 iske saath hi digital pement kii seva dene vaale sabhi bainkon ko phising atake se apane network ko bachaane ke liye sabhi jaruri kadam jald se jald uthaane ke nirdesh die gaye hai
 According to the Reserve Bank, with the decision to move the country towards digital India and cashless economy, a large number of first time users will use these mediums
 isse bainkon ke network or graahakon ke acount par bada khatra paidaa ho saktaa he
 Therefore, the Reserve Bank has cautioned all banks not to leave any scope for negligence and as soon as problems arise, to prepare a framework for immediate redressal
 sabhi bank or digital pement sansthaaen in adeshon kaa sahi dhang se paalan kar rahe hai yaa nahin yah sunishchit karne ke liye rigerv bank ne unhen 21 disambar tak department of pement and setelment ko apana vistrut plan saunpane ke liye kaha he
 In this, they will also have to give the name and time of the auditor to get their network audited
 rigerv bank ke mutabik 500 rupee or 1000 rupee kii karency ko band karne ke baad se desh main online pement or cashles tranjaction kaa chalan teji se bad rahaa he
 In such a situation, if cyber attack or fraud on banks or other digital payment platform can stop our move towards cashless economy
 kya hoga is audit membank ordigital pement placeformka audit karne vaali companiyaan unke hardware dhaanche, oparating system or critical programs kaa baariki se adhyayan karengi
 Audit companies will also ensure that the bank's online payment gateway, communication platform of ATM machines, security of point of sale machines are maintained and updated
 iske saath hi is audit main yah bhi tay hoga ki kya bainkon ne suraksha ke liye sabhi jaruri kadam uthaae hai yaa nahin
 It also includes their recovery in the event of an accident or cyber attack and training the staff to deal with any situation

 Taking a lesson from the 2013 natural disaster in Uttarakhand, the government has finalized the redevelopment plan to surround Kedarnath Dham in the most sensitive mountain area of the state with a three-wall security shield
 kendriya awaas evam shahari maamalon ke mantralay dwaara taiyaar kii gai kedarpuri purnirmaan yojana ke sanshodhit masaude main dharmik evam aitihaasik mahatv ke is tirthasthal ko prakritik aapadaaon se sthaayee suraksha pradaan karne ke upaay kiye gaye hai
 a ministry official said that with the approval of Prime Minister Narendra Modi, three important changes have been incorporated in the revised scheme
 inamen kedarnath mandir parisar ko teen stareey suraksha kavach se gherna, saadhakon kii aadhyatmik sadhana ke liye kedarnath dham ke aasapaas pahadiyon main guphaayen bananaa or tirthayatriyon ke rukne thaharne sahit kisi bhi makasad se hone vaale nirmaankaryon ko nadi ke bahaav kii disha main hi karne kii baadhyataa ko shaamil kiya gaya he
 In the earlier plan it was said that the temple complex should be surrounded by two-tier security shield of the walls
 ullekhneey he ki pichley mahinemodi ne kedarnath mandirke aasapaas do varg kimi kshetrafal main 750 karod rupee kii punarnirmaan yojana ko hari jhandi dikhaai thi
 After the amendments made to the scheme at his suggestion, the Ministry has finalized it
 iske tahat kedarnath dham ko angreji varnmaala ke 'you' akshar ke aakaar kii teen deevaaron se gheraa jaayegaa
 In this, the first wall of Boulder in 'U' shape will be built on both sides of the temple, enclosing the entire complex parallel to the stream of Mandakini and Saraswati river
 iske baad doosraa gheraa dhaatu kii jaaliyon ke kavach vaali pattharon kii diwaar kaa or teesraa gheraa kancreet kii diwaar kaa hoga
 In the earlier plan, a two-tier security ring was to be built
 teen stareey suraksha ghere se bhavishya main baadh, bhuskhalan, bukamp jaisi aapadaa se pracheen mandir ko surakshit bananaa he
 Also, the pilgrims' unhindered access to the flow of water will be limited by making several ghats on the banks of the Saraswati and Mandakini rivers on both sides of the shrine
 punarnirmaan yojana main donon nadiyon ke kinare tirthayatriyon ke rukne thaharne or anya suvidhaon ke liye jameen kii sataha se nirdhaarit oonchai par hi nirmaankarya sunishchit kiya jayega
 Each building will be constructed in the direction of the river
 samudratal se lagbhag 11 hajaar foot kii oonchai par sthit kedarnath dham ke liye sanshodhit punarnirmaan yojana main paryaavaran evam paristhitikeey tantra kii chintaaon kaa puraa dhyaan rakhaa gaya he
 Also, two monitoring towers will be built in Chorabari area to monitor the weather
 yojana ke tahat imaaraton ko banane main sthaneey nirmaan saamagree or vaastu se judi paaramparik takanic kaa istemaal karne kii baat kahi gai he
 It has been proposed to make low-height buildings up to a maximum of two storeys
 saath hi mandir parisar main mukhya imaarat ke chaaron ore 50 meter ke daayre main koi bhi nirmaankarya nahin hoga, jisase nirmaankarya kii vighnbaadha se mukt rakhane ke liye samooche parisar ko puri tarah se khulaa rakhaa ja sake
 Its purpose is to avoid a situation like panic
 ullekhneey he ki har saal lagbhag chah lakh tirthayatri kedarnath ke darshan ke liye jate hai
 In the revised plan, a provision has also been made to construct caves and a museum around the temple premises for meditation and meditation practice
 lagbhag 1500 karod rupee kii laagat vaali is yojana ko rajya sarkaar kii bhagidaari se paanch saal main puraa karne kaa lakshya tay kiya gaya he
